ea:["$","p",null,{"className":"x:not-first:mt-6 x:leading-7","children":"Rewrite regex literals into shorter, consistent, and safer form (character-class shorthands, redundant ranges)."}]
eb:["$","p",null,{"className":"x:not-first:mt-6 x:leading-7","children":["Each regex literal is optimized the way ",["$","a",null,{"href":"https://github.com/DmitrySoshnikov/regexp-tree","target":"_blank","rel":"noreferrer","className":"x:focus-visible:nextra-focus x:text-primary-600 x:underline x:hover:no-underline x:decoration-from-font x:[text-underline-position:from-font]","children":[["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"regexp-tree"}],false]}]," canonicalizes it: character classes collapse to their shorthands (",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"[0-9]"}]," → ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"\\d"}],", ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"[^A-Za-z0-9_]"}]," → ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"\\W"}],"), ranges are deduplicated and sorted, flags are alphabetized, and redundant quantifiers merge (",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"\\s?\\s?\\s?"}]," → ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"\\s{0,3}"}],"). The autofix replaces the whole literal, except when it is the object of a ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":".source"}]," or ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":".toString"}]," member access — those are reported without a fix so a serialized-source consumer is not rewritten under it. Literals carrying the ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"u"}]," or ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"v"}]," flag are skipped, matching upstream, because ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"regexp-tree"}]," does not handle Unicode / Unicode-sets mode reliably. A ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"new RegExp(\"pattern\", \"flags\")"}]," string constructor rewrites its pattern argument through the same character-class shorthands; the rewritten pattern keeps the argument’s original quote character and is re-escaped for it, so a pattern carrying a newline, a control character, or the delimiter quote comes back as a valid string literal."]}]

36d:["$","p",null,{"className":"x:not-first:mt-6 x:leading-7","children":["The rule only reports when a ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"String.raw"}]," template would reproduce the value exactly, so a literal is left alone when it carries any escape other than ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"\\\\"}]," (",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"\"\\\\d\\t\""}]," would turn its tab into the two characters ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"\\t"}],"), when its value ends with a backslash (a raw template cannot end in one), when it contains a backtick or ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"$${"}]," (the template would close early or interpolate), or when a line continuation spreads it over two lines. A no-substitution template is reported under the same value-preserving condition, except that its newlines are already literal, so a multi-line template stays reportable; the quasi of a tagged template — including ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"String.raw`…`"}]," itself — is never reported. The report carries no autofix."]}]

3a1:["$","p",null,{"className":"x:not-first:mt-6 x:leading-7","children":["The established ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"unicorn/prevent-abbreviations"}]," ID is retained for configuration compatibility. 3a2:["$","p",null,{"className":"x:not-first:mt-6 x:leading-7","children":["A binding is diagnosed once at its declaration. One collision-free replacement is autofixed across every reference, while ambiguous replacements are editor suggestions. Bindings declared with a named ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"export"}]," modifier, plus ambient, cross-file-merged, JSX tag, ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":".vue"}]," source, parameter-property, and attached-JSDoc ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"@param"}]," bindings, remain diagnostic-only because a source-only rename cannot safely preserve their external names or references. A local binding re-exported through an export list remains fixable because the fixer preserves the external spelling (",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"export { err }"}]," becomes ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"export { error as err }"}],"). Default-export local names can likewise change without changing the external ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"default"}]," name. The conservative ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":".vue"}]," gate protects template references that are outside TypeScript’s source-file AST."]}]
